    <string name="ddl_create_photo_grouping_view" formatted="false">"CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS photos_month_grouping AS SELECT MIN(_id) * -1 AS _id, -1 AS photo_id, MAX(photo_date) AS photo_date, 0 AS user_id, 0 AS family_id, '' AS photo_uri, '' AS photo_hash, 0 AS width, 0 AS height, 0 AS fav, 0 AS reg_date, 0 AS is_active, '' AS session_id, '' AS feed_content, 0 AS upload_status, CAST(STRFTIME('%Y', photo_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS year, CAST(STRFTIME('%m', photo_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS month, COUNT(*) AS count FROM photos GROUP BY year, month UNION ALL SELECT _id, photo_id, photo_date, user_id, family_id, photo_uri, photo_hash, width, height, fav, reg_date, is_active, session_id, feed_content, upload_status, CAST(STRFTIME('%Y', photo_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS year, CAST(STRFTIME('%m', photo_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS month, 0 AS count FROM photos ORDER BY photo_date DESC, _id;"</string>
    <string name="ddl_create_photo_table">CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS photos ( _id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, photo_id INTEGER DEFAULT 0, photo_date INTEGER NOT NULL, user_id INTEGER NOT NULL, family_id INTEGER NOT NULL, photo_uri TEXT NOT NULL, photo_hash TEXT UNIQUE, width INTEGER DEFAULT 0, height INTEGER DEFAULT 0, fav INTEGER DEFAULT 0, reg_date INTEGER NOT NULL, is_active INTEGER NOT NULL, session_id TEXT, feed_content TEXT, upload_status INTEGER DEFAULT 0, exif_gps_latitude REAL, exif_gps_longitude REAL, UNIQUE (photo_hash) ON CONFLICT REPLACE );</string>
    <string name="ddl_create_video_grouping_view" formatted="false">"CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS videos_month_grouping AS SELECT MIN(_id) * -1 AS _id, 0 AS video_id, MAX(video_date) AS video_date, 0 AS reg_date, 0 AS length, 0 AS tier, '' AS video_object_name, '' AS thumbnail_object_name, '' AS feed_content, CAST(STRFTIME('%Y', video_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS year, CAST(STRFTIME('%m', video_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS month, COUNT(*) AS count FROM videos GROUP BY year, month UNION ALL SELECT _id, video_id, video_date, reg_date, length, tier, video_object_name, thumbnail_object_name, feed_content, CAST(STRFTIME('%Y', video_date, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS year, CAST(STRFTIME('%m', video_date,' unixepoch', 'localtime') AS INTEGER) AS month, 0 AS count FROM videos ORDER BY video_date DESC, _id;"</string>

    <string name="library_MergeAdapter_libraryDescription">MergeAdapter accepts a mix of Adapters and Views and presents them as one contiguous whole to whatever ListView it is poured into. This is good for cases where you have multiple data sources, or if you have a handful of ordinary Views to mix in with lists of data, or the like.
